GT Equivalence Verification (CRK2)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidate formulas: 217

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
f(A)= -0.19494483384724354\,A \;+\; 0.24819026785686927\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of \(t\) after parameter choices, (ii) contain a linear \(-kA\) term with \(k=0.1949448338\ldots\), and (iii) contain exactly \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) with amplitude \(0.2481902678\ldots\). In particular, candidates whose only non-polynomial nonlinearity is \(\cos(A\cdot\text{const})\), \(\sin(\cdot)\), \(\exp(\cdot)\), rational functions, powers, \(\log(Ac+1)\) (without cosine), etc., cannot be made equal to \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) for all \(A\).

Below, each candidate is checked against these structural necessities.

---

### 1
\(A c_0 + A c_1 e^{c_2 t} + \frac{c_3}{A c_4+c_5}+c_6 e^{c_2 t}+c_7\).  
Can remove \(t\) by \(c_1=c_6=0\) (or \(c_2=0\)), but remaining terms are linear + rational + constant. No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No.**

### 2
Sum of terms all over \((A^3+c_1)\) with some \(e^{A c_3}\). Even if exponentials set to 0, it’s rational in \(A\). Cannot equal \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) term. **No.**

\(A^{c_0}c_1\sin(Ac_2+c_3)+c_4\cos(Ac_5)\).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK2)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidates evaluated: 217
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: `-0.19494483384724354*A + 0.24819026785686927*cos(log(A + 1))`**

Note that `_w = 1.27313...` and `c1 = 0.19494...`, so `c1*_w = 0.24819...`.

The GT has two components:
1. A linear term in A: `-0.195*A`
2. `cos(log(A + 1))` term

Let me analyze each candidate for structural compatibility. The key question is whether each candidate can produce both a linear term in A AND a `cos(log(A+1))` term.

**Key observations:**
- `cos(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function
- It cannot be represented by polynomials, exponentials, rational functions, `sin(A)`, `cos(A)`, `log(A+1)`, `exp(A)`, or combinations thereof
- Only candidates containing `cos(log(...))` or `sin(log(...))` (with phase shift) can potentially match

Let me scan for candidates with `log` inside trigonometric functions or vice versa:

**Candidate 49:** `c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(A) + 1) + c4)`
- With A ≥ 0: `c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*A + 1) + c4)`
- Set c2=1, c3=1, c4=π/2: `c0 + c1*cos(log(A + 1))`
- But GT also needs `-0.195*A`. There's no A term here. We need the linear term.
- **Cannot match** - missing linear A term.

**Candidate 26:** `A*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*sin(c4*log(c5*Abs(A) + 1) + c6))`
- Has `A*c0` for the linear term, but the transcendental part is `exp(sin(log(...)))`, not `cos(log(...))`. These are structurally different.
- **Cannot match.**

**Candidate 63:** `c0*exp(A*c1) + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*Abs(A) + 1) + c6)`
- With A ≥ 0: Set c1=0 to kill exp → constant. Then: `(c0+c2) + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*A+1) + c6)`
- Set c4=1, c5=1, c6=π/2: `const + c3*cos(log(A+1))`
- But no linear A term! Setting c1=0 removes the only source of A-dependence besides the sin term.
- **Cannot match.**

**Candidate 199:** `c0 + c1/(A*c2 + c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A*c7 + c8*t) + 1) + c9)`
- Set c1=0 (kill rational term), c8=0 (kill t): `c0 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*|A*c7| + 1) + c9)`
- No linear A term. **Cannot match.**

**Candidate 213:** `A*c0 + c1 + c2*log(c3*exp(c4*sin(A*c5 + c6*t + c7)) + 1)`
- Has A*c0 but the second part is `log(exp(sin(...)) + 1)`, not `cos(log(...))`. **Cannot match.**

**Candidate 172:** `A*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*cos(c4*log(c5*exp(c6*t) + 1)*sin(A*c7 + c8)))`
- Very complex, but the argument structure doesn't yield `cos(log(A+1))`. **Cannot match.**

After exhaustive search, **no candidate** contains the structure `cos(log(A + c))` or `sin(log(A + c))` combined with a linear A term. Candidate 49 has `sin(log(...))` which can become `cos(log(...))` via phase shift, but lacks the linear A term.
